<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i>Zelfstandig naamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b>barre</b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li>horizontaal rondhout aan de muur voor balletoefeningen</li>
<li>legger op een brug, gebruikt voor gymnastiekoefeningen</li></ol>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:bars.html>bars</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bærs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fish.html>fish</a>, perch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*barsaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">perch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prickly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:barvrouw.html>barvrouw</a> (44125)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:basiliek.html>basiliek</a> (58109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:basket.html>basket</a> (4578)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord_2"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
